name:B‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçj‚Äça‚Äçm‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äç ‚ÄçS‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äç.
info:Family suite
info:Stayed in December 2021
info:Family
info:40 Reviews
rating:3.2
posted:Posted December 28, 2021
msg:Thank you Ocean Sonic but we have to say farewell and will not come back. 

We (a family with three children) have been to the Ocean Sonic for the second time. First in 2016 we were really happy with our Family Suite and the overall great services everywhere in the hotel. 

Now we came back after five years because we hoped to have again a good time. The location is still very good but the hotel and its services have aged. The room not in best condition anymore. Furnitures and facilities (especially bathroom) was quite old and doesn‚Äôt look good anymore. The hotel gave us this time another room layout with sea view (last time we had garden view over two floors) but the family suite was old. The receptionist could only speak Chinese and at our arrival the counter was overwhelmed by the number of guests which made our checkin quite lengthy. 

The breakfast was in the past a real highlight with a lot of good food and a balanced mixture between international and good Chinese food. Now it focused much more on the Chinese guests (which is reasonable in times with fewer foreign guests) but the quality, variety and services also suffered compared to 2016. Individual food stations have been reduced to a minimum and most food is now pre-cooked. The coffee machine was able to provide also cappuccino but often 2 of 4 coffee machines were broken and the queues for the remaining ones were long. The coffee machine and the buffet in the children breakfast area were not in service.

The Sanya Bay is in my eyes still the best place to go because the beach is great and the waterline isn‚Äôt steep. The waves are reasonable high and can be managed well with younger children. Around the  hotel you can find many restaurants but mostly only seafood. After 1 week seafood our children were looking for variety but all other restaurants like good Russian restaurants have shutdown.

Overall, the price and the service is still okay-ish for the Ocean Sonic. But now you can find many good alternatives in the Sanya Bay with good prices as well. We will try one of these during our next winter stay in Sanya. 
----------------------------------------

msg:Great location opposite beach. Balinese buildings - feels like you are in Bali.  Great breakfast! Something for everyone, coffee from a machine, pastries, toast, yoghurt, coconut milk dessert with jelly, egg and so much more! Noodle station plus all kinds of cooked food. I loved the fish. 
Breakfast catered well to us and we are foreigners.

Pool area was lovely with great kids facilities, 2 water slides, an inflatable toy to climb and jump off and various large toys to rent at the pool.  Pool towels provided.

Bubble party in afternoon.
 
Small playroom.

Walking distance to some local restaurants which specialised in seafood but had other dishes. 

Our room was affordable with a living room and a bedroom with 2 large single beds. Small cot was provided for my baby.
My kids slept in the living room as the couch as it was so large.

Excellent value for a family. 

Beach across road was great for families with young kids and they had day beds to lie on and beach toys for my baby. 

Ladies sell fresh fruit while you are on the beach too.

There is a nearby set of shops walking distance if you walk left of hotel about 7 minutes towards the city. You will see some restaurants, turn left and there are more restaurants on the right. Downstairs we found a local air conditioned food court which had ice fruit smoothies served in a bowl. They were delicious!

You can also get these delivered to the hotel. Add a staff member on wechat when you check in and this helps immensely with everything you need. They helped me add someone who spoke English.

msg:The Ocean Sonic Resort was one of the worst overnight experiences I‚Äôve endured in many years. Given that my last ‚Äúhotel‚Äù involved sleeping in a tent in the Himalayas with a blanket for a door in subzero temperatures, that‚Äôs really saying something. I had seen the deceptively pretty pictures of the Ocean Sonic Resort on Trip.com, and foolishly booked a non-refundable 3-night stay for Christmas. My experience at the Ocean Sonic was so terrible, I was happy to waste thousands of yuan to flee to another hotel, rather than staying there for longer than one night. This hotel threatened to ruin my holiday.

The Ocean Sonic is a run-down facility long overdue for renovation, and chock full of very bad ideas. The room decor is a depressing wood panel more suitable for a 1970s college dorm room. The toilet is shockingly low to the floor, guaranteed to injure a few thigh muscles every time you squat. Want to take a bath? The tub is- and I can‚Äôt make this up- on the balcony! And while you bathe, you‚Äôll have plenty of folks staring at you, because the only other views from the ‚Äúdeluxe ocean view‚Äù rooms are rusty roofs filled with trash, and an abandoned hotel next door. So your neighbors are far more entertained by your nude body in the tub. Muzak- really BAD Muzak, where the singers mispronounce the words-blasts in the hallway outside your room, 24/7, making it impossible to sleep. This is the only hotel in China where they want to charge you for a (usually complimentary) tea bag. 

The resort‚Äôs restaurants are barely open for business, except for breakfast, which is overrun by hordes of shoving pushy guests obviously near starvation. While trying to find food at other times within the resort, I was directed to closed restaurants no less than three times. The indifferent staff didn‚Äôt seem to be aware that those businesses weren‚Äôt open. At breakfast, my table was outside, in the rain with no umbrella. Luckily, there is a food store on site at the Ocean Sonic, part of a complex billed by the resort as a ‚ÄúShopping Mall,‚Äù even though the only other store in this ‚Äúmall‚Äù is a women‚Äôs clothing boutique. There are practically no other dining options in the area; only four identically mediocre seafood restaurants a quarter mile away, where your potential dinner sits in fish tanks staring at you. 

I could go on, but you get the idea. Until somebody gets rid of the rude staff (notable shout out to Haj, the sole hard working employee who seemed to care), and sinks $15-$20 million into upgrading the facilities, the Ocean Sonic Resort should be your LAST RESORT for staying in Sanya. Keep heading down the road and choose from countless other excellent hotels nearer downtown Sanya with better ocean views, superb service, luxurious rooms, and edible food. Want to stay closer to the airport? Try the MGM Grand. When I fled the Ocean Sonic, I chose the JW Marriott. 

Consider yourself warned.

It is close to the airport, so you don't have to get up early to catch the plane, and you can sleep comfortably! It is close to the scenic spots, so traveling is worry-free and labor-saving! A few steps to the left from the hotel entrance is the bus stop, which can go to Tianya Haijiao, Xidao, Nanshan Cultural Tourism Zone, Xiaodongtian and other scenic spots, which is very convenient. Go out of the hotel gate and cross the road to the right to take the bus on the opposite side. You can go to the downtown attractions of Sanya and Yalong Bay and Haitang Bay. The distance is a bit far. If you don't want to take the bus, you can take a taxi or rent a car, which is also a good choice. Across the road from the hotel is the beach coconut forest coconut dream corridor. It is very nice to take pictures of the sunset in the evening! Our trip happened to be low tide on the first day of the new year. The children dug various hermit crabs in the small holes on the beach, which was very interesting. After the waves receded, they could also pick up large clams and starfish. The weather was hot and the children were playing in the hotel swimming pool and didn't want to get up no matter how much they shouted. Our exclusive butler Xiao Long is very considerate. Environment: On the beach, opposite Internet celebrity attractions. I really like the balcony view, it's very comfortable. I'm afraid of the sun, so I spend most of my time on the balcony watching the sea. There were no bugs in the room. The room the housekeeper arranged is very satisfactory. I also called before checking out to ask if I need a late check out. it's actually very good. When checking in and checking out, there will be doormen to help with luggage, and the cleaning staff will also replace supplies in time to ensure sufficient mineral water. The uncle who watered the flowers in the morning would greet me warmly, very happy~ Overall, the service is very good.
Location: Very close to the airport, we arrived early in the morning, so we chose this hotel based on the principle of proximity. The hotel is also very close to the beach. Just go through the underpass. There are elevators up and down the underground passage, which is very convenient. And there are not many people on the beach in front of the hotel, which is more than a hundred times better than the Coconut Dream Corridor. I am in Yalong Bay now, and I feel that the sand here is similar to the sand on the beach in front of Haiyun Hotel, and the clarity of the sea water is not much different.
Facilities: There are places where you can rest everywhere in the hotel, which is very good. There is a public swimming pool downstairs and a children's area. There are also supermarkets and clothes shops inside the hotel, but the prices are slightly more expensive. Food can be ordered on takeaway, but you have to go to the takeaway area of the hotel to pick it up.
Breakfast: very rich! The breakfast is very complete, both Western and Chinese. Every day, there will be Baoluo powder or Hainan powder with Hainan characteristics, which tastes good. The fruit is also very fresh, the soy milk and milk are very pure, and the bread and snacks are also delicious. Opposite the restaurant is the children's restaurant, and you can shuttle back and forth between the two restaurants.
Room: After all, it is an old hotel, the floor of the room and the countertop of the sink will have some traces of use. But the room is very clean and the view is very good. For us, the traces of use can be ignored. It's just that the mattress is not very comfortable to sleep on, it's soft, and there is a sound when you turn over.
In the end, I am very happy to choose Haiyun, and I will come again if I have the opportunity in the future. Thanks to every service staff! Thank you!

Facilities: You can eat, drink, and have fun, and you have to pay extra for billiards.
Overall evaluation: An old hotel with a good location, convenient, and price, compared with luxury hotels in Sanya, it is still more affordable. All in all, it is recommended.
